This was my second time using Precision Temperature for AC repair and maintenance. I'm extremely pleased with the work that was performed. My first repair in October 2020 was by a technician named Carlos and my second repair was in May 2021 by a technician named Marco. Both technicians took the time to explain in detail what the issues were, how the system is supposed to function, and what it would take to repair. I really appreciated them taking the time to answer all of my questions above and beyond. Both were extremely professional, respectful and on time. They also completed the work quickly and correctly, spending extra time making sure everything was secured, sealed and protected. On my second repair, I needed an entire new breaker box for my AC. Marco did a great install and it really looked nice when it was finished. He even made sure it was properly sealed and within code. I have been extremely satisfied with both repairs and will continue to use Precision Temperature exclusively for my HVAC needs thanks to Carlos and Marco's extreme professionalism, attention to detail and the knowledge they provided me as a homeowner. Bree was also great at taking my appointment request and answering all my my questions and concerns, she was very friendly and helpful and did her best to find me the earliest appointment possible.</review>

This is a really good park but on weekends parking can be scarce. There is a large field that is rented out for children's soccer and football leagues and there is a really nice fenced in playground. This is technically private property so there is almost always a security guard nearby. There is also a trail running along the back of the park that lets you experience how the property was before it was developed. We go there a lot but, parking can definitely be a problem.< /text>

<user>109485411642398929869</user><name>Nate Brewer< /name><Date>1468014576279</Date><rate>5</rate>< Review>
Positives:
-there are two gates, both on one side of the park where there are always guards to ensure no kid wanders off on their own
-no sand, sawdust, or other nasty park dirt that comes home in the car and into the house
-rubber padding underneath the entire structure
-the swings actually work here (most new swings slow kids down and require excessive pushing/pumping)
-the kids love the structure and always find other kids to play with
-areas to sit in the shade or sun and a nice grassy area to sit as well
-rumor has it the park is regularly sterilized!
-bathrooms are always stocked and reasonably clean for park bathrooms and all have changing tables
-great mix of people from all over and most are pretty chill
-there are usually a fair amount of dads or male caregivers with children at the park (as a stay at home dad, this can be important)
-always entertaining to watch the games on all sides of the park (soccer, tennis, basketball, and baseball/softball)

Negatives:
-the rubber padding can be hot to the feet on hot days so socks or shoes may be required
-parking lot can fill up during sporting events or when the neighboring school is being let out, but street parking is almost always available
-due to the proximity to the ocean and marina, it can get windy and cool down rather quickly, especially as evening approaches<//Review>

< review>
My car buying experience was great at American Motors. Ali was extremely helpful and the whole process couldn't have been easier. I found the car online and decided to come by to check it out. I usually stay away from smaller dealerships, but I'm glad I didn't this time.

The car was in amazing shape, the interior was spotless, the engine bay was so clean, and everything checked all the boxes I was looking for in a commuter car. I knew I wanted a diesel, and Ali informed me that with the huge diesel scandal, a lot of cars got recalled and have a 4 year 45k mile warranty. I looked this up, searched the VIN on Audi's website, and confirmed this was all correct.

There was never any pressure into buying a car, I never felt rushed, and Ali even held the car for me with a deposit because I was closing on my house and needed some time before returning.

All in all, great service and great little selection of cars.

I'll be sending my friends over if they see a car they like.< /review>

< review>
The only reason I am giving this place one star is because I can't give it a zero star, which is what it deserves. Cafe Rosarita is pretty good /ok for a  quick (rather small) meal. They have $5.50 LUNCH "special" platter; choice of 1 of 3 ( either a beef taco or a chicken taco or a cheese enchilada, with each including beans/rice.
Every day they have 1 menu item on special pricing, which is an $ amount less than the regular price for that item on any other given day. The Interior; open space, lotsa tables /no booths, outdated(not modern), but very decorated. :) The guitar music is fantastic, Love it. Overall it's ok but for the prices of most plates, it's not a lot of food, I'm thin & I never take  any back home. It's cool to try a different plate each time. Chips & Salsa are good/ tastes fresh.< /review>

< review>
This was my first time ever having to go through the expungement process, and I must say I am extremely pleased with the experience.  I saw alot of reviews on this company and alot of the complaints I saw were of people complaining of the documentation they had to provide. I feel you get what you put in and this company is here to help you as much as you let it. That being said, before I even called I had a copy of my disposition ready to go. I took the eligibility test, sent an email and got a response within hours. I personally talked to Mr. Huffman, got a list of things I needed to get ready and got to work.  Even living in Texas, the process went by smooth and quick.  Mr. Huffman required a few documents I already had ready prior and I was able to get letters of recommendation immediately.  Again, some of the complaints I saw were of people expecting this company to do ALL the work completely for them, which I thought was a bit absurd, especially living in these times we're in full of restrictions and delays. My start date was 03 DEC 2020 and I got my record Expunged with paper work in by 05 APR 2021. Not bad for being 3 states over and not once having to go back to California for any reason.  Mr. Huffman kept me updated with both emails and their tracking system online.  If you are going to go with this company, just remember, YOU are hiring them, and they are only as effective as you let them be. So have all your ducks in a row and be ready to help with some paperwork in order to receive the fastest response times available. Thank You Mr. Huffman for everything, I can now push forward with my career.</review>

< text>
This place is small space-wise, menu-wise, and TV wise. I'm kind of confused about what they're going for.

The space isn't that big a deal. The menu only offers 4 burgers, and 2 kinds of fries. They do offer blackbean burgers as option. The kitchen staff is quick and the food we did get was delicious.

More disappointing is that their beer selection is tiny! There is only 4 beers on tap, but each beer well selected. They have a similarly small wine selection. And a decent liquor selection.

There were a good number of people  watching the Stanley Cup hockey game, but the TVs were small. The space had some interesting atmosphere, but a lot of blank dark painted walls too.

So honestly, I don't know what this place is going for and I'm not sure they know either. I enjoyed my burger, fries, and beer but I feel like I've seen everything this place has to offer after one visit. Maybe I'd go back if it were cheaper but they charge brewery prices for to little in my opinion. Its worth a try if you've never been

Edit: A lot of people are saying this place has the best burger in town. Not even close. Burgers are 7/10 at best. The bar in SD is high<//text>

< Text>
I can see why this place has been in business for decades, the burgers are amazing and probably have to be in the top 3 in San Diego I've had thus far. This place is a dive bar with decor from yesteryear and you can easily drive past without ever knowing it was there. I believe I've had the best barbecue bacon cheeseburger of my life here. The bun's a crazy soft and the bbq sauce and burger had great flavor. I've also had the taco/burger which was also great. If you're looking for a solid burger, go here.<//Text>

< text>
This is a must try in San Diego! The portion size is average which is great if you are trying to fill your burger needs. I ordered a Balboa Burger and the California Burgito . The Balboa has a great taste, the beef is very juicy and high quality. The tomatoes and lettuce are very crisp, topped of with soft buns and fresh aioili house sauce. The Kennebec fries are great since they have little bit of spice. It was a very original take on burgers and it exceeded my expectations. The location its self is a hole in the wall but it definitely shines when being introduced to the traditional bar decor. Kevin the person helping us out was very professional and on top of it. I would recommend to come early on the weekdays because I could totally see this place being very popular on the weekends. Overall I would highly recommend The Balboa... Pro tip everyday from 4-6pm The Balboa burger is $5. What a steal. Hope they keep this promotion.</text>

<Rating>5</Rating><text>Hole in the wall dive bar with one heck of a good burger!
Heard about this place from many friends who believe The Balboa has one of, if not the, best burgers in San Diego.
After trying many other spots (Hodads, Rocky's, The Friendly, etc.), I can truly say that they do indeed make my Top 10 list. Only reason they didn't make the Top 5 was that I don't put anyone in the Top 5 unless I've tried their burger multiple times.
The burger is flat-top grill cooked, served on a soft fresh traditional bun with lettuce, tomato, onions, cheese and their secret zesty aioli sauce.
DON'T expect a super clean restaurant style  place, this is a transitional dive bar and keeps it real.</text>< pictures>

< Text>
What an amazing spot! I am not surprised that its a local favorite. I did not try any other burger joints in SD, but this is by far the best burger I have had. Although I have to be honest I haven't had many.

The place is in a very quiet neighborhood, it was very close to our airbnb. It doesn't look like much from the outside but its what inside that matters - burgers!!! We went on a Monday night and there where still people there. Its quite dimly lit, have about 5-6 tables and bar seating.

Now about the food. The burgers are amazing!! Me and my husband both had their balboa burger and it was just perfect! The patty was dripping! I was using the wrap they give with the burger and still ended up with juices on my hands. The bun is perfectly toasted and adds a charred flavor to the burger. The toppings are simple some onions, tomatoes and their sauce which is bomb! We both inhaled our burgers. The drinks were really nice too. I got their cucumber punch and it was really refreshing, nice break from the meaty burger. We got garlic fries on the side and these were one of the most well seasoned fries I have had in a restaurant. So good!! Service was quick and easy.

Would highly recommend to all meat-lovers. Also tip: you can get an extra patty if you are extra hungry.</Text>

<Time>1573949553932< /Time></record></dataset><record>
<Text>Balboa Bar & Grill is a dive bar that serves the best burgers in San Diego, bar none. Everything about Balboa Bar & Grill's's burgers, including the beef mixture ratio, the secret garlic aioli recipe, and even their brand of mustard, has been purposefully and uniquely chosen to deliver a transcendent and congruent burger experience where the whole is much greater than the mere sum of its parts, but the most impressive unique feature are their buns, which are freshly-baked bolillo rolls shaped like hamburger buns. Some San Diegans may recognize bolillo as the same French-lilke Mexican bread used to make molettes and tortas in households and restaurants around the region.

And, yes, the other reviews you'll read about the delicious garlic fries are on point -- but I usually find myself ordering the regular fries made of the same Kennebec potatoes which are just as nice and crispy, but allow me to actually open my mouth around other people later in the evening without melting their faces.

In short, this is THE place to get burgers in San Diego.</Text><rate>5</rate><Name>Jay Keyes< /Name>< pictures>

<Text>I am not very familiar with downtown San Diego. From the surface and not knowing any better, this doesn't seem like a part of town you want to hang around, especially once the sun goes down. The Balboa is small. There is a bar with probably a dozen-ish stools and then maybe 8 dinning tables. I could be off by 1 or 2 in my count. Anyways, the service was great and the bartender was very friendly. The Balboa Burger was excellent, I highly recommend and I would happily eat it again. The Garlic Fries, not so much. They weren't terrible but they weren't good. I guess I would use the word eatable to describe them. The place is very dark. When you enter during daylight, you will need a few minutes for your eyes to adjust so you can see. I felt like the pricing was very fair for what I received. No table side service, you need to order at the bar counter. This is not really a family place. So maybe leave the kids home. I would go back and I would recommend.< /Text>< pics>

<userid>115576115272002931559< /userid><name>Annette FitzGerald<//name>< time>
1525216646833< /time>
< Rating>
5< /Rating>
< review>
Places like this restore your faith in humanity: dark, hole-in-the-wall atmosphere, rock-n-roll on the stereo, great burgers cooked to perfection, a small but absolutely solid selection of beer, and real cocktails made with an actual helping of booze--not some corporate spudder from a nozzle pre-measured to exactly one ounce.

The staff are great, the owner is cool, and it has the feel of a local pub rather than a joint catering to tourists--if my husband and I were local we would be in this place every day. As it is, we will be dropping in whenever we have a hankering for San Diego's fine martime air.< /review>

4<//Rate>
< Text>
So I've been to Tin Can Ale House a handful of times as a performer and spectator and never had the 'pleasure' of having a Dood Food burger. Well, last night I was starving and was going to see a show there so I figured I'd break my Dood Food celibacy and take the plunge. The place was PACKED, so it took a while for my order to be ready. I'd say 'bout a half hour or so.

I ordered the BBQ Burger and garlic fries. Awe man! That burger made me wanna slap my momma and my grandma (God bless her soul). That tasty meat puck was did a tango on my taste buds and had me beggin for mercy. The juicy patty was dropping sauce and grease like it was hot...and it was hot. Fresh. Soft bun. Sauteed onions. It was THAT good, but not THE best. The garlic fries had fresh minced garlic...none of that powdery business. Tasty.

Overall, this experience was good. I'm ready to go back and have another variety and see if the legend lives on.</Text>

<Review>It seems they no longer offer a happy hour :(

If you check the Google reviews of this restaurant, you'll notice that "happy hour" the top keyword mentioned and probably weighs heavily into the older ratings.

I'm kind of torn because I was on an emotional roller coaster watching Balboa's original location almost close, then come back even bigger. I called and they said they've done away with their happy hour menu which is kind of disappointing because their regular prices have gone up a fair amount.

I understand the pandemic situation and that restaurants have struggled this past last year, but it seems like a lot of places are too good to offer any kind of incentives to loyal regular customers anymore.

The burgers are great for purists who don't want a sauced-up, condiment-laden burger that hides the quality of the meat. Are they worth regular menu price? For me, I don't know -- I want to support the Balboa but now it seems an out-of-reach luxury I might have to regrettably pass on in the future.<//Review>< Pics>
None< /Pics>
